Environment and forests Department
Declaration of Myladumparai Forest Block Bit-17, 28, 29 
and 30 in Andipatti Taluk, Theni (Previously in Madurai 
District.) as Reserved Forest under the Tamil Nadu 
Forest Act.
[G.O. Ms. No. 28, Environment and Forests (FR.14), 
20th March 2018, Г°Ж’В°Q 6, В«ГЅMГ·вЂ№H, FВјГµЕ“ГЂГµЛњ

No.II(2)/EF/663/2018.вЂ”In exercise of the powers 
conferred by Section 16 of the Tamil Nadu Forest Act, 1882 
(Tamil Nadu Act V of 1882), the Governor of Tamil Nadu 
hereby declares that the area, within the boundaries of 
which are specified in the Schedule below as reserved 
forest with effect on and from the 06-03-2019.
The schedule

: 	 Theni (Previously in

Block
boundaries
Bit-17вЂ“Survey Field Number 214вЂ“4.830 ha.
North.-The boundary of the Forest Block starts from the 
tri-junction point of Survey Field Numbers 212, 213 and 214 
of No.22, Myladumparai Village, the boundary runs towards 
east along the southern side of Survey Field Numbers 213 
and 181 till it meets the tri-junction point of Survey Field 
Numbers 181, 180 and 214 of the said Village.
East and South.-Thence, the boundary turns towards 
south along the western side of Survey Field Number 180 
and it turns towards western north direction along the 
common boundary between Survey Field Numbers 170 and 
214 and till it meets the tri-junction point of Survey Field 
Numbers 212, 170 and 214.
West.-Thence, the boundary turns towards north along the 
eastern boundary of Survey Field Numbers 212 and it turns 
towards east along the common boundary between survey 
Field Numbers 212 and 214 till it meets the starting point.
ADMITTED вЂ‰вЂ‰RIGHTS
Right No.1:вЂ“The Thar road leading from Myladumbarai 
Village reserved forest Survey Field Number 214 Via Kumanan 
Tholu and Joints Arasaradi road Myladumparai Village Bit 
No.17, Survey Field Number 214 starts from the south 
west in the metre of 62.8 and 50.2 and reach from north 
east corner in the metre of 156.60 and 113.00 metre, Total 
distance of 283.60 metre, width of the road is 8.00 metre.

No.II(2)/HWMP/664/2018.вЂ”The Governor of Tamil Nadu 
having been satisfied that the lands specified in the 
schedule below are acquired under Tamil Nadu Road Sector 
Project-II Highways purpose to wit for upgrading Arcot to 
Villupuram road (SH 04) at Km 29/800 to Km 110/200 and 
Km 113/200 to Km 114/600 in Muttathur Village, Vikkiravandi 
Taluk, Villupuram District and it has already been decided 
that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for 
the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled and 
managed by the Divisional Engineer, Tamil Nadu Road Sector 
Project вЂ“II, Tiruvannamalai and after having considered 
the cause shown by the owner or other person having 
interested in the said lands, as the case may be, do hereby 
issue and publish the following notice under sub-section 
(1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 
(Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu 
Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the wet ands specified 
in the scheduled below and measuring to an extent of 
1636 Sq.mtrs. in S.No.62/2A2 and etc., in Muttathur Village, 
Vikkiravandi Taluk, Villupuram District to the same, a little 
more or less needed for TNRSP-II, Highways purpose to 
wit for upgrading Arcot to Villupuram Road (SH 04) at 
Km. 29/800 to Km. 110/200 and Km. 113/200 to Km. 114/600.
The plan of the lands under acquisition are kept 
in the office of the Special District Revenue Officer 
(Land Acquisition), Tamil Nadu Road Sector Project-II, 
Chennai вЂ“ 28 and Special Tahsildar (L.A), Tamil Nadu Road 
Sector Project-II, Tiruvannamalai and may be inspected at 
any time during office hours.

No.II(2)/HWMP/665/2018.вЂ”The Governor of 
Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified 
in the schedule below are acquired for Highways Purpose 
to wit for widening Trichengode вЂ“ Paramathi Road (SH-86) 
in Pillakalathur Village, Paramathi Velur Taluk, Namakkal 
District and it having already been decided that the entire 
amount of compensation to be awarded for the land is to be 
paid out of the funds controlled and managed by Highways 
Department after considering the cause shown by the owner 
or other persons having interest on such lands as the 
case may be do hereby publish the following notice under 
sub section 1 of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways 
Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act, No. 34 of 2002).

NOTICE
Under sub-section 1 of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu 
Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the 
schedule below and measuring to an extent of 60 sq.mtrs 
of dry lands in S.No. 265/1A2 and 265/10B in Pillakalathur 
Village, Paramathi Velur Taluk, Namakkal District to the 
same, a little more or less required for Highways purpose 
for widening (SH 86) Trichengode вЂ“ Paramathi Road.
The plan of the lands is kept in the office of the 
Special District Revenue Officer (Land Acquisition), 
Tamil Nadu Road Sector Project-II, Salem and may be 
inspected at any time during office hours.

No.II(2)/HWMP/666/2018.вЂ”The Governor of Tamil Nadu 
having been satisfied that the lands specified in the 
schedule below are required for Highways purpose to wit 
for widening of Nanguneri Road (SH 89) from Km. 0/000 
to Km 35/200 in Thisaiyanvilai Village, Radhapuram Taluk in 
Tirunelveli District and it having already been decided that 
the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the 
lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed 
by the Divisional Engineer (Highways), Tamil Nadu Road 
Sector ProjectвЂ“II, Tirunelveli after considering the cause 
shown by the owner or other person having interest in 
the said lands as the case may be do hereby publish the 
following notice under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the 
Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the 
Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 
2002), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the 
dry lands specified in the Schedule below and measuring 
to an extent of 678 Square Metres in Thisaiyanvilai Village, 
Radhapuram Taluk in Tirunelveli District to the same, a 
little more or less needed for TNRSP-II Highways purpose, 
to wit for widening of Nanguneri Road (SH 89) from Km. 
0/000 to Km. 35/200.
The plan of the lands under acquisition is kept 
in the Office of the Special District Revenue Officer 
(Land Acquisition), Tamil Nadu Road Sector Project-II, 
Trichirappalli and the Special Tahsildar (Land Acquisition), 
Tamil Nadu Road Sector Project-II, Tirunelveli and may be 
inspected at anytime during office hours.

No.II(2)/HWMP/667/2018.вЂ”The Governor of 
Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in 
the Schedule below are acquired under TNRSP-II Highways 
purpose, to wit for strengthening and widening of Tirunelveli-
Tenkasi Road (SH-39) from Km. 47/000 to Km. 50/600 in 
Gunaramanallur Village, Tenkasi Taluk in Tirunelveli District 
and it having already been decided that the entire amount 
of compensation to be awarded for the acquisition of lands 
is to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed 
by the Highways Department and after having considered 
the cause shown by the owner or other persons having 
interest in the said lands, as the case may be, do hereby 
issue and publish the following notice under sub-section 
(1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 
(Tamil Nadu Act, 34/2002)
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the 
Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 
2002), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the 
dry lands specified in the Schedule below and measuring 
to an extent of 242 Square Metres in Gunaramanallur 
Village, Tenkasi Taluk in Tirunelveli District to the same, a 
little more or less needed for TNRSP-II Highways purpose, 
to wit for strengthening and widening of Tirunelveli-Tenkasi 
Road (SH-39) from Km. 47/000 to Km. 50/600. 
The plan of the lands under acquisition is kept in 
the Office of the Special District Revenue Officer (Land 
Acquisition), Tamil Nadu Road Sector Project-II, Tiruchirapalli

No.II(2)/HWMP/669/2018.вЂ”The Governor of Tamil Nadu 
having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule

wit for widening of Tirunelveli-Tenkasi Road (SH-39) from

No.II(2) /HWMP/671/2018.вЂ”The Governor of Tamil Nadu 
having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule 
below are acquired for Highways purpose to wit for Minor 
junction improvement in Oddanchatram - Dharapuram вЂ“ 
Tiruppur Road (SH-37) in Dharapuram Municipality and 
Suriyanallur Village, Dharapuram Taluk, Tiruppur District

compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out 
of the funds controlled and managed by Divisional Engineer 
(Highways) Tamil Nadu Road Sector Project-II, Tiruppur 
and after having considered the cause shown by the owner 
or other persons having interest on such lands as the case 
may be, do hereby publish the following notice under sub-
section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 
(Tamil Nadu Act, 34 of 2002)
NOTICE
	
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the 
Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 
2002), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the 
Rayathu dry and R.manai lands specified in the Schedule 
below and measuring to an extent of 945.4 Square 
Metres in S.No.9/1B etc., for the purpose of Minor junction 
improvement in Oddanchatram - Dharapuram вЂ“ Tiruppur

Village, Dharapuram Taluk in Tiruppur District.

the office of the Special District Revenue Officer (Land 
Acquisition), Tamil Nadu Road Sector Project-II, Salem and 
Special Tahsildar (L.A), Tamil Nadu Road Sector Project-II, 
Tiruppur and may be inspected at any time during office

No. II(2)/HO/672/2018.вЂ”In exercise of the powers 
conferred by the proviso to sub-section (1) of Section 11 
of the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1973 (Central Act 2 of 
1974), the governor of Tamil Nadu, after consultation with 
the High Court, Madras, hereby establishes a Special Court 
of Judicial Magistrate at Tirunelveli in Tirunelveli District to 
try the offences punishable under Negotiable Instruments 
Act, 1881 (Central Act XXVI of 1881).

S. krishnan,
	
Principal Secretary to Government.
labour and employment department
Notifications under the Minimum Wages Act.
Revision of Minimum rates of Wages for the Employment 
in Sea Food Processing Industry under the Act.
G.O. (2D) No. 66, Labour and Employment (J1), 2nd July 2018, 
ГќQ 18, MГ·вЂ№H, FВјГµЕ“ГЂГµЛњ ГќвЂЎВґ-2049.]
No. II(2)/LE/674/2018.вЂ”In exercise of the power conferred 
by clause (b) of sub-section (1) of Section 3 and sub-section 
(2) of Section 5 of the Minimum Wages Act, 1948 (Central 
Act XI of 1948) and in supersession of the Labour and 
Employment Department Notification No. II(2)/LE/303/2013, 
published at page 250 and 251 of Part II вЂ” Section 2 of the 
Tamil Nadu Government Gazette, dated the 10th April 2013, 
the Governor of Tamil Nadu after consultation with the 
Advisory Board, hereby revises the minimum rates of wages 
payable to the classes of employees in the employment in 
Sea Food Processing Industry in the State of Tamil Nadu, 
specified in column (1) of the Schedule below, as specified 
in the corresponding entries in column (2) thereof, the draft 
of the same having been previously published as required by 
clause (b) of sub-section (1) of Section 5 of the said Act. 
2.	
This notification shall come into force with effect 
on and from the date of its publication in the Tamil Nadu 
Government Gazette.

Explanations.-	(1)	 Dearness Allowance.вЂ“ In addition to the 
above minimum rates of basic wages, 
the employees shall be paid dearness 
allowance as follows:- 
(i) 	 The dearness allowance shall be linked to the 
Average Consumer Price Index Number for Chennai 
City for the year 2010 (that is 161 points with base 
2001=100) and for every rise of one point over 
and above 161 points, an increase of Rs.30.80 
(Rupees Thirty and paise eighty only) per month 
shall be paid as dearness allowance. 
(ii) 	The dearness allowance shall be calculated on 
the first April of every year on the basis of the 
average of the indices of the preceding twelve 
months, that is, from January to December. 
(iii) 	The first calculation shall be effective from the 
date of publication of this Notification in the 
Tamil Nadu Government Gazette based on the 
Average Consumer Price Index of the previous year. 
(2) 	Where the nature of work is the same, no distinction 
in the payment of wages shall be made in the case of 
men and women employees. 
(3) To arrive at the daily rates of wages, the monthly 
wages shall be divided by 26. 
(4) 	Wherever the existing wages are higher than the 
minimum wages fixed herein. such existing wages shall be 
continued to be paid.
Draft Notification regarding the Revision of minimum rates 
of wages for the employment in Handloom Weaving 
Industry under the Act.
[G.O. (2D) No. 68, Labour and Employment (J1), 3rd July 2018, 
ГќQ 19, MГ·вЂ№H, FВјГµЕ“ГЂГµЛњ ГќвЂЎВґ-2049.]
No. II(2)/LE/675/2018.вЂ”The following draft of Notification, 
which is proposed to be issued in exercise of the powers 
conferred by clause (b) of sub-section (1) of Section 3 
and sub-section (2) of Section 5 of the Minimum Wages 
Act, 1948 (Central Act XI of 1948), is hereby published 
for information of all persons likely to be affected thereby, 
as required by clause (b) of sub-section (1) of Section 5 
of the said Act. 
2.	
Notice is hereby given that any objection or 
suggestion, which may be received from any person with 
respect thereto, on or before the 16-10-2018, will be 
considered by the Government of Tamil Nadu. Objection 
or suggestion, if any, should be addressed to the Principal 
Secretary to Government, Labour and Employment Department, 
Secretariat, Chennai-600 009 through the Commissioner of 
Labour, Chennai-600 006. 
Draft Notification. 
In exercise of the powers conferred by clause (b) 
of sub-section (1) of Section 3 and sub-section (2) of 
Section 5 of the Minimum Wages Act, 1948 (Central Act XI 
of 1948) and in supersession of the Labour and Employment 
Department Notification No.II(2)/LE/182/2013, published at 
pages 142 to 159 of Part II-Section 2 of the Tamil Nadu 
Government Gazette, dated the 13th February 2013, the 
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby revises the minimum rates 
of wages payable to the employees in the employment in 
Handloorn Weaving Industry in the State of Tamil Nadu 
in respect of the works specified in column (2) of the 
Schedule below as. specified in the corresponding entries 
in column (3) thereof.
The Schedule
Employment Handloom Weaving Industry.

Extra Wages: 
Dhoti.- Extra wages shall be paid for the extra work. 
The rate of extra wages vary from 5% to 15% or even 
more on the basic wages depending upon the size of the 
pettu border design. 
Sarees.- Extra wages shall be paid for the extra 
work. The rate of extra wages vary from 5% to 20% or 
even more on the basic wages depending upon the Merit/
Technique involved in the extra work (Border, Butta and 
Mundhi design etc.,) 
Explanations.- (1) Dearness Allowance.- In addition 
to the minimum wages fixed above, dearness allowance 
shall be paid as indicated below:- 
	
(i) 	 Dearness allowance shall be paid at the rate 
of 10% of the basic wages plus extra wages linked with the 
productivity from the date of publication of this Notification 
in the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette. 
	
(ii) 	 Additional increase of 5% on the prevailing 
basic wages plus extra wages shall be granted every year 
on the 1st April till the next revision. 
(2) Where the nature of work is the same no distinction 
in the payment of wages shall be made between men and 
women employees.
(3) Wherever the existing wages are higher than the 
minimum wages fixed herein, the same shall be continued 
to be paid.
Draft Notification regarding the Revision of minimum 
rates of wages for the employment in Food Processing 
Industry under the Act.
[G.O. (2D). No. 70, Labour and Employment (J 1),
10th July 2018, ГќQ 26, MГ·вЂ№H, FВјГµЕ“ГЂГµЛњ ГќвЂЎВґ-2049.]
No.II(2) /LE/676/2018.вЂ”The following draft of a Notification 
which is proposed to be issued in exercise of the powers 
conferred by clause (b) of sub-section (1) of Section 3 
and sub-section (2) of Section 5 of the Minimum Wages 
Act, 1948 (Central Act XI of 1948), is hereby published 
for information of all persons likely to be affected thereby, 
as required by clause (b) of sub-section (1) of Section 5 
of the said Act. 
2. Notice is hereby given that any objection or 
suggestion, which may be received from any person with 
respect thereto, on or before 16-10-2018 will be considered 
by the Government of Tamil Nadu. Objection or suggestion, 
if any, should be addressed to the Principal Secretary to 
Government, Labour and Employment Department, Secretariat, 
Chennai-600 009 through the Commissioner of Labour, 
Chennai - 600 006. 
Draft Notification. 
In exercise of the powers conferred by clause (b) of 
sub-section (1) of Section 3 and sub-section (2) of Section 5 of 
the Minimum Wages Act, 1948 (Central Act XI of 1948) and 
in Supersession of the Labour and Employment Department 
Notification No. II(2)/LE/478/2014 published at pages 
534-537 of Part II - Section 2 of the Tamil Nadu Government 
Gazette, dated the 13th August 2014, the Governor of 
Tamil Nadu hereby revises the minimum rates of basic wages 
payable to the classes of employees in the employment in 
Food Processing industry in the State of Tamil Nadu as 
specified in column (2) of the schedule below, as specified 
in the corresponding entries in columns (3) and (4) thereof.

Aug. 1, 2018]	
TAMIL вЂ‰NADU вЂ‰GOVERNMENT вЂ‰GAZETTE	
	
	
вЂѓ 733
Explanations.-
(1) Classification of Zones.- 
Zone A and B shall comprise of the following areas:- 
Zone A : All Municipal Corporations.
Zone B : All areas other than the areas of Municipal 	
	
    Corporations. 
(2) Dearness Allowance.- In addition to the minimum 
rates of basic wages fixed above, the employees shall be 
paid dearness allowance as indicated below:- 
	
(i) 	 The dearness allowance is linked to the 
Average Chennai City Consumer Price Index for the year 
2010, that is 161 points (with base 2001=100) and for 
every raise of one point over and above 161 points, an 
increase of Rs.36.00 (Rupees thirty six only) per month 
shall be paid as dearness allowance. 
	
(ii) 	 The dearness allowance shall be calculated 
'on the first April of every year on the basis of the average 
of the indices for the preceeding twelve months, that is 
from January to December. 
	
(iii) 	The first calculation shall be effective from the 
date of publication of this Notification in the Tamil Nadu 
Government Gazette based on the Average Chennai City 
Consumer Price Index Number for the previous year. 
(3)  (i) To arrive at the daily rate of wages, the monthly 
rate of wages shall be divided by 26. 
	
(ii) To arrive at the monthly rate of wages, the 
daily rate of wages shall be multiplied by 30. 
(4) 	Where the nature of work is the same, no distinction 
in the payment of wages shall be made in the case of 
male and female employees. 
(5) 	Wherever the existing wages are higher than the 
minimum wages fixed herein, the existing wages shall be 
continued to be paid.
Disputes between Workmen and ManagementsвЂ‰вЂ‰referred 
to Industrial Tribunal for Adjudication.

cЛњГµЕ“Г™Лњ AГіВЈГ±Л†Fв„ў ГћГІЖ’A ГµВјвЂ№ ГґВЈЛњГЄВЎ & Г‡Е В«ГіВЈ 
LIВЄГ¬вЂ  ECC  ГҐЛњвЂљГєВЈЕ  ГўВЎГё GЛњГµВЈГЁЛ†FЕёВ°вЂ№, cЛњГµЕ“Г™Лњ

ГЄЖ’ГЁвЂ№ ГўВЎГё ВЄГ®ВЈNЕёГЄЖ’ГЁЛ†FЕёВ°IВ¬Г¬В«ГІ ГЎFГІ Г ГІЛњВѕ Г±ЕёГЃвЂ№

ГўВЎГЃ ГњГіВІ ГЁВјВ¶ГµГ®ВЈВЅвЂ№;

ВЄГЄГІГґВЈ? ГќвЂ№ ГўQв„ў,  Г KГІ Г Л†Г®ГіВѕГЁЕ“ HГёЕ HвЂљГЁ.

В¶В¬Гё, 22 В«Г± 2018, В¬ГµГЁВЈC 8, MГ·вЂ№H, FВјГµЕ“ГЂГµЛњ 
ГќвЂЎВґ-2049.]
No. II(2)/LE/680/2018.вЂ”ГћвЂ°Г® ГќВ¬Г­JВЎ ГћВ¬Г­Е Hв„ў 
В°PЕ HвЂ ВґЕ“Г· ВЄГ°ВЈВјЕ“ ВЄГ®ВЈГ¬ЛњГ°ВЈГЁ ГЁВЈвЂ¦CВ№ГівЂ№ Г±ВЈГµвЂ Г¬вЂ№, 
ГҐГіГЁГ¬вЂ№ 
CЕ ГЁВЈвЂ  
ГћвЂЎГ¬vвЂ KГІв„ў 
вЂљВ«ГіВЈЛ† 
ВЄГЄВЎГ¬Kв„ў 
ГњВ¬Г±вЂ°В¶Е“Г· ГЋQЕ HГіv ГћвЂ°FГІВЈ HВ¬ГіВ«ГµвЂ  LIВЄГ¬вЂ  ГўВЎГё 
GЛњГµВЈГЁЛ†FЕёВ°вЂ№ ГЋQЕ HГіv ГћвЂ°FГІВЈ ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·ЛњГЁЕ“ ГЄЖ’ГЁвЂ№ 
ГўВЎГё ВЄГ®ВЈNЕёГЄЖ’ГЁЛ†Fв„ў Г ГЃЕ HГ№ГіВЈГЁ Г Е“Г· FВј. K. В°Г±В«ГіГЄВЎ 
ГўВЎГё ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈOвЂљВ°вЂ№ ГћВ¬Г¬В«ГІ ВЄГ®ВЈNЕёГ®ГЁГіВЈГЃ ГўВївЂ°В¶Е“Г·В¶ 
ГўВЎГЃ ГњГіВІ ГЁВјВ¶ГµГ®ВЈВЅвЂ№;
В«Г±ЕёВЄГЄВЈВЎГ№ Г®ГЁГіВЈВ¬Гё ВЄГЄВЎВ¬Г№, ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·Лњ cFГ±ВЎГёЛ†FВЎ 
bЛњMЕёГЁВЈГЁ ГњГ‚Е В№ГµВ¶ ГњГµCГІВЄГ±ВЎГЃ Г®IвЂєГЇВЈВґ ГќГЂГЇЛњ 
ГњГµЛњГЁЕ“ ГЁВјВ¶ГµГ®ВЈВЅвЂ№;
1947-ГќвЂ№ ГќвЂЎВґ ВЄГ®ВЈNЕёГ®ГЁГіВЈГЃГЁЕ“ ГЄвЂ Г¬Л†FВЎ (Г±Л†FГІ 
ГЄвЂ Г¬вЂ№ XIV/1947) 10(1)(c) HKMВЅвЂ№, 10(1)(d) HKMВЎ ГµГівЂ№В№ 
GГ°вЂ°Г®В¬Г№JВЅвЂ№ 
ГµГ¶Ж’AВ»Е“Г· 
ГњFГЁВЈГіЖ’ГЁВ¬Г·вЂљ 
ВЄГЁВЈвЂЎВґ, 
Г®IвЂєГЇВЈВґ ГќГЂГЇЛњ ГњГµЛњГЁЕ“ В«Г±ЕёВЄГЄВЈВЎГ№ Г®ГЁГіВЈГЃ, ВЄГЄВЎВ¬Г№, 
ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·Лњ cFГ±ВЎГёЛ†FВЎ bЛњMЕёГЁВЈГЁ ГњГ‚Е Г°Е Г°Г¬ В«ГµвЂЎВґвЂ№ 
ГўВЎГЃ ГћГ®Г№ВЈв„ў ГќВ¬Г­JВґAГёВЈЛњ.

11-03-2015 ГЇВЈOвЂ Г¬ ГЁВ®Г®Л†FВЎ ГЌГґвЂ№ Г¦ГіВЈвЂЎВґ Г®В°FГЁВЈвЂЎ

GЛњГµВЈГЁЛ†FВЎ ВЄГЄГІв„ў, 1947вЂ‰вЂ‰ГќвЂ№ ГќвЂЎВґ ВЄГ®ВЈNЕё Г®ГЁГіВЈГЃ ГЄвЂ Г¬Е

26-02-2015 ГЇВЈOвЂ Г¬ ГЁВ®Г®Л†FВЎ ГЌГґвЂ№ Г¦ГіВЈвЂЎВґ Г®В°FГЁВЈвЂЎ 
Г°ВјГµвЂ№ ВєВ®ГµВ¬Г¬В»вЂ№ ВєВЎГ№В«Гі Г°EcвЂљГЁвЂ№ ВЄГЄЕ’Г® В«Г±ЕёГ°В® 
GЛњГµВЈГЁЛ†FВЎ ВЄГЄГІв„ў, 1947-ГќвЂ№ ГќвЂЎВґ ВЄГ®ВЈNЕёГ®ГЁГіВЈГЃ ГЄвЂ Г¬Е  
HKВѕ 33-Г¤ ePГІ ВЄГЄГІГґВЈ ? ГќвЂ№ ГўQв„ў,  Г KГІ Г Л†Г®ГіВѕГЁЕ“ 
HГёЕ HвЂљГЁ.

GЛњГµВЈГЁЛ†FЕёВ°вЂ№ ГЋQЕ HГіv ГћвЂ°FГІВЈ ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·ЛњГЁЕ“ ГЄЖ’ГЁвЂ№ 
ГўВЎГё ВЄГ®ВЈNЕёГЄЖ’ГЁЛ†Fв„ў Г ГЃЕ HГ№ГіВЈГЁ Г Е“Г· FВј. R.вЂ‰вЂ‰ГіВ«Г±wГ°ВЈВ№ 
ГўВЎГё ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈOвЂљВ°вЂ№ ГћВ¬Г¬В«ГІ ВЄГ®ВЈNЕёГ®ГЁГіВЈГЃ ГўВївЂ°В¶Е“Г·В¶ 
ГўВЎГЃ ГњГіВІ ГЁВјВ¶ГµГ®ВЈВЅвЂ№;

ГќвЂ В«Г¬ВЈВ«Г±Г»ВЎ HВ¬ГіВ«ГµвЂ  LIВЄГ¬вЂ  ГўВЎГё GЛњГµВЈГЁЛ†FЕёВ°вЂ№, В№FГІ 
ГјГ№ГЇВЈГІГЁ ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·Лњ ВєВЎГ№E ГћвЂЎВЄГ¬вЂљГіВЈ ГќвЂ В«Г¬ВЈВ«Г±Г»ВЎ 
ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·ЛњГЁЕ“ AВ¬Г· ГўВЎГё ВЄГ®ВЈNЕёГЄЖ’ГЁЛ†FЕёВ°IВ¬Г¬В«ГІ 
ВЄГ®ВЈNЕёГ®ГЁГіВЈГЃ ГўВївЂ°В¶Е“Г·В¶ ГўВЎГЃ ГњГіВІ ГЁВјВ¶ГµГ®ВЈВЅвЂ№;
В«Г±ЕёВЄГЄВЈВЎГ№ Г®ГЁГіВЈВ¬Гё ВЄГЄВЎВ¬Г№, ВЄГ®ВЈNГґВЈГ·Лњ cFГ±ВЎГёЛ†FВЎ

В«Г°ВЈвЂљВ°ГµГіЛ†В¶вЂљ ГЁГ¶ГЁвЂ№ (MВїЕ В№ГівЂ№) LIВЄГ¬вЂ , MВїЕ В№ГівЂ№
